  notifications:
    +---n wsa-client-event
    |  +--ro client-mac?                   yang:mac-address
    |  +--ro wtp-mac?                      yang:mac-address
    |  +--ro state-transition-timestamp?   yang:date-and-time
    |  +--ro audit-session-id?             string
    |  +--ro ssid?                         string
    |  +--ro client-event?                 wsa-types:wsa-client-events
    |  +--ro client-event-result?          wsa-types:wsa-client-event-result
    |  +--ro vlan-id?                      uint32
    |  +--ro client-vnid?                  uint32
    |  +--ro client-sgt?                   uint16
    |  +--ro rssi?                         int8
    |  +--ro snr?                          uint8
    |  +--ro ms-ap-slot-id?                uint8
    |  +--ro mm-client-role?               wireless-mobility-types:mm-client-role
    |  +--ro ipv4-address?                 inet:ipv4-address
    |  +--ro ipv6*                         inet:ipv6-address
    |  +--ro dhcp-server-ip-addr* []
    |  |  +--ro server-ip?   inet:ip-address
    |  +--ro aaa-server?                   inet:ip-address
    |  +--ro is-fabric-client?             boolean
    |  +--ro client-event-reason?          wsa-types:wsa-client-event-reason-3p
    |  +--ro client-event-reason-addon?    wsa-types:wsa-client-event-reason-addon-3p
    +---n rogue-events
       +--ro reporting-ap
       |  +--ro name?          string
       |  +--ro mac-address?   yang:mac-address
       |  +--ro slot-id?       uint32
       +--ro rogue-mac-address?                   yang:mac-address
       +--ro (event-type-choice)?
          +--:(rogue-potential-honeypot-detected)
          |  +--ro potential-honeypot-detected
          |     +--ro ssid?      string
          |     +--ro channel?   uint32
          +--:(rogue-potential-honeypot-cleared)
          |  +--ro potential-honeypot-cleared
          |     +--ro ssid?      string
          |     +--ro channel?   uint32
          +--:(rogue-ap-impersonation-detected)
          |  +--ro ap-impersonation-detected
          |     +--ro impersonating-src-mac?   yang:mac-address
          |     +--ro is-beacon-ds?            boolean
          |     +--ro channel?                 uint8
          +--:(rogue-mfp-containment-detected)
             +--ro pmf-info-detected
                +--ro is-client?        boolean
                +--ro pmf-client-mac?   yang:mac-address

KPI for model: openconfig-wifi-phy.yang
module: openconfig-wifi-phy
  +--rw radios
     +--rw radio* [id]
        +--rw id           -> ../config/id
        +--rw config
        |  +--rw id?                       uint8
        |  +--rw operating-frequency?      identityref
        |  +--rw enabled?                  boolean
        |  +--rw transmit-power?           uint8
        |  +--rw channel?                  uint8
        |  +--rw channel-width?            uint8
        |  +--rw dca?                      boolean
        |  +--rw allowed-channels*         oc-wifi-types:channels-type
        |  +--rw dtp?                      boolean
        |  +--rw dtp-min?                  int8
        |  +--rw dtp-max?                  int8
        |  +--rw antenna-gain?             int8
        |  +--rw scanning?                 boolean
        |  +--rw scanning-interval?        uint8
        |  +--rw scanning-dwell-time?      uint16
        |  +--rw scanning-defer-clients?   uint8
        |  +--rw scanning-defer-traffic?   boolean
        +--ro state
        |  +--ro id?                             uint8
        |  +--ro operating-frequency?            identityref
        |  +--ro enabled?                        boolean
        |  +--ro transmit-power?                 uint8
        |  +--ro channel?                        uint8
        |  +--ro channel-width?                  uint8
        |  +--ro dca?                            boolean
        |  +--ro allowed-channels*               oc-wifi-types:channels-type
        |  +--ro dtp?                            boolean
        |  +--ro dtp-min?                        int8
        |  +--ro dtp-max?                        int8
        |  +--ro antenna-gain?                   int8
        |  +--ro scanning?                       boolean
        |  +--ro scanning-interval?              uint8
        |  +--ro scanning-dwell-time?            uint16
        |  +--ro scanning-defer-clients?         uint8
        |  +--ro scanning-defer-traffic?         boolean
        |  +--ro base-radio-mac?                 oc-yang:mac-address
        |  +--ro dfs-hit-time?                   oc-types:timeticks64
        |  +--ro channel-change-reason?          identityref
        |  +--ro total-channel-utilization?      oc-types:percentage
        |  +--ro rx-dot11-channel-utilization?   oc-types:percentage
        |  +--ro rx-noise-channel-utilization?   oc-types:percentage
        |  +--ro tx-dot11-channel-utilization?   oc-types:percentage
        |  +--ro counters
        |     +--ro failed-fcs-frames?   oc-yang:counter64
        |     +--ro noise-floor?         int8
        +--rw neighbors
           +--ro neighbor* [bssid]
              +--ro bssid    -> ../state/bssid
              +--ro state
                 +--ro bssid?             oc-yang:mac-address
                 +--ro ssid?              string
                 +--ro rssi?              int8
                 +--ro channel?           uint16
                 +--ro primary-channel?   uint16
                 +--ro last-seen?         oc-types:timeticks64
